    <script>
    (function replaceRedirectNotificationData () {
        if (('hash' || 'search') in window.location) {
            var isShown = !!window.location.hash.match(/#redirect/) || window.location.search.match(/rdt/);
            var dataEl = document.getElementById('redirect-notification-data');
            var data = JSON.stringify({ isShown: isShown });
            try {
                jQuery(dataEl).text(data);
            } catch (e) {
                dataEl.text = data; // IE8
            }
            if (isShown) {
                if ('replaceState' in window.history) {
                   var search = window.location.search;
		   		   var indexofredirectionFromType = search.indexOf('rdt');
		   		   var indexOfAmp = search.indexOf('&', indexofredirectionFromType);
		   		   var clearedPath;
		   		   var replaceIndex = (indexOfAmp == -1) ? (search.length - 1) : indexOfAmp;
		   		   clearedPath = search.replace(search.substring(indexofredirectionFromType, replaceIndex + 1), '');
             window.history.replaceState('', document.title, window.location.pathname + clearedPath.replace(/[?&]$/, ''));
                } else {
                    window.location.href = '';
                }
            }
        }
    }());
    </script>

                            deliveryMessageUrl : "/shop/delivery-message",
                            geoLookupUrl : "/shop/address/geo-lookup",
                            omnitureData: [window.s.pageName, "Step 1"],
                            doSendLeadQuoteMetric: true
                        });
                });

                var loadDeferedImages = function () {
                    window.removeEventListener('scroll', loadDeferedImages);
                    var pxroValue = jQuery.cookie('pxro');

                    jQuery('img[data-defer-src]').each(function() {
                        var el = jQuery(this);
                        var deferSrc = el.attr('data-defer-src');
                        var scaleParam = el.attr('data-defer-scaleparams2');

                        if (pxroValue === "2" && scaleParam && deferSrc.indexOf(scaleParam) === -1) {
                            var srcPre = deferSrc.slice(0, deferSrc.lastIndexOf('?') + 1);
                            deferSrc = srcPre + scaleParam;
                        }
                        el.attr('src', deferSrc).removeAttr('data-defer-src');
                    });
                };
                window.addEventListener('scroll', loadDeferedImages);

                window.addEventListener('load', function() {
                    loadDeferedImages();

                    if(window.as.AnimateOnScroll) {
                        window.as.AnimateOnScroll.init();
                    }
                });
            </script>

                                            aria-expanded="{{#question-8}}true{{/question-8}}{{^question-8}}false{{/question-8}}">
                                            <span class="as-accordion-title">
                                                What does “SIM-free” mean?
                                            </span>
                                            <span class="icon icon-plus as-accordion-plusicon"></span>
                                        </button>
                                    </h3>
                                </div>
                                <div 
                                    data-render="materializer" 
                                    data-uid="question-8" 
                                    id="question-8" 
                                    data-show-height="computed" 
                                    data-hide-height="0" 
                                    class="ase-materializer ase-materializer-show" 
                                    {(data-shown)}="question-8" 
                                    >
                                    <div class="as-accordion-content row">
                                        <div class="as-accordion-box-content column large-10 small-12">
                                                    “SIM-free” means your iPhone doesn’t ship with a carrier nano-SIM. The SIM-free iPhone sold on apple.com and at the Apple Store is unlocked. That means you can use a nano-SIM or eSIM from any carrier that provides service for iPhone.<sup>*</sup>
<br />
<br />
If Sprint is your carrier, you’ll need to get a new nano-SIM card in order to activate your iPhone XS, iPhone XS Max, or iPhone XR.
<br />
<br />
<sup>*</sup> Use of eSIM requires a wireless service plan (which may include restrictions on switching service providers and roaming, even after contract expiration). Not all carriers support eSIM. Use of eSIM in iPhone may be disabled when purchased from some carriers. See your carrier for details. To learn more, visit <a href="https://support.apple.com/kb/HT209044" target="_blank">https://support.apple.com/kb/HT209044</a>.
                                        </div>
                                     </div>
                                </div>

                                                    eSIM technology allows you to add a cellular plan to your iPhone without using a nano-SIM card. Activating an eSIM will require scanning a valid QR code distributed by a wireless carrier, or signing up for a participating plan through a wireless carrier app.<sup>*</sup>

<br />
<sup>*</sup> Use of eSIM requires a wireless service plan (which may include restrictions on switching service providers and roaming, even after contract expiration). Not all carriers support eSIM. Use of eSIM in iPhone may be disabled when purchased from some carriers. See your carrier for details. To learn more, visit <a href="https://support.apple.com/kb/HT209044" target="_blank">https://support.apple.com/kb/HT209044</a>.

                                <div class="as-accordion-title-container">
                                    <h3 class="as-accordion-header">
                                        <button 
                                            class="as-accordion-button {{#question-13}}as-accordion-isexpanded as-accordion-item-isexpanded{{/question-13}}"

                                            <span class="as-accordion-title">
                                                Which capacity is right for me?
                                            </span>
                                            <span class="icon icon-plus as-accordion-plusicon"></span>
                                        </button>
                                    </h3>
                                </div>
                                <div 
                                    data-render="materializer" 
                                    data-uid="question-13" 
                                    id="question-13" 
                                    data-show-height="computed" 
                                    data-hide-height="0" 
                                    class="ase-materializer ase-materializer-show" 
                                    {(data-shown)}="question-13" 
                                    >
                                    <div class="as-accordion-content row">
                                        <div class="as-accordion-box-content column large-10 small-12">
                                                    iPhone XS comes in three capacities: 64GB, 256GB, and 512GB. The term “GB” stands for gigabytes. The more gigabytes you have, the more content you can store on your iPhone, such as apps, games, photos, HD videos, music, and movies. If you have a large music or photo library or lots of apps, it’s a good idea to consider an iPhone with a larger capacity. If you rarely download apps or you don’t take many photos or videos, an iPhone with a smaller capacity may be better for you.
                                        </div>

                                </div>

                            <li class="as-accordion-item">
                                <div class="as-accordion-title-container">
                                    <h3 class="as-accordion-header">
                                        <button 
                                            class="as-accordion-button {{#question-14}}as-accordion-isexpanded as-accordion-item-isexpanded{{/question-14}}" 
                                            data-ase-materializer="question-14" 
                                            data-ase-click="toggle" 
                                            aria-controls="question-14" 
                                            aria-expanded="{{#question-14}}true{{/question-14}}{{^question-14}}false{{/question-14}}">
                                            <span class="as-accordion-title">
                                                When I buy from apple.com, does my iPhone come ready to use?
                                            </span>
                                            <span class="icon icon-plus as-accordion-plusicon"></span>
                                        </button>
                                    </h3>
                                </div>
                                <div 
                                    data-render="materializer" 
                                    data-uid="question-14" 
                                    id="question-14" 
                                    data-show-height="computed" 
                                    data-hide-height="0" 
                                    class="ase-materializer ase-materializer-show" 
                                    {(data-shown)}="question-14" 
                                    >
                                    <div class="as-accordion-content row">
                                        <div class="as-accordion-box-content column large-10 small-12">
                                                    <p>If you completed the carrier activation steps for AT&amp;T, Sprint, T-Mobile or Verizon when you purchased your new iPhone online, it will arrive ready to use. Just turn it on and follow the onscreen instructions to set it up. If you chose to skip carrier activation at the time of purchase, you’ll need to contact your wireless carrier or visit an Apple Store to enable cellular services. You can also set up your iPhone without a nano-SIM using Wi-Fi. You will need an active nano-SIM to enable cellular services.</p>
<p>If you selected the SIM-free iPhone, you’ll need to insert your own nano-SIM card or obtain one from the supported carrier of your choice and activate it in order to use cellular services on your iPhone. If Sprint is your carrier, you’ll need to get a new nano-SIM card in order to activate your iPhone XS, iPhone XS Max, or iPhone XR.</p>

                                        <div class="as-accordion-box-content column large-10 small-12">
                                                    <p>Just answer a few questions online or in an Apple Store regarding the condition of your iPhone. We’ll provide either an estimated trade-in value or a simple way to recycle it.</p>
<p>If you’re trading in online, we’ll apply your estimated trade-in value to the purchase of your new iPhone. Then we’ll send you a trade-in kit (at no cost to you) so you can send us your device. Once we receive your trade-in device, a team will inspect it and verify its condition. If the condition matches what you described, there’s nothing more you need to do. If it doesn’t match, your original payment method will be charged the difference in value. In that case, we’ll work with you to confirm that you still want to move forward with the trade-in.</p>
<p>If you accept the trade-in estimate in the store, we’ll give you instant credit toward a purchase.</p>
<p>And if you choose to recycle your device, we’ll either handle it in the store or provide a prepaid shipping label so you can send your device to our accredited recycling partner.</p>

                                                <h3 class="as-community-mostusefulanswer">Best Answer:</h3>

                                                    <span class=" {{#answers-1}}as-hide{{/answers-1}} ">Yes, as long as you have the earpod/headphone lightning connector.</span>
                                                </div>

<a href="/shop/question/answers/iphone/is-the-iphone-x-s-max-waterproof/QX2XY94P449K4U4UX"   class="as-community-questiontitle">Is the iPhone X s max waterproof?</a>                                                <ul class="as-community-statistics">
                                                    <li>
                                                        <span class="fn">Asked by Rafael S from Vila Velha </span>
                                                    </li>
                                                    <li class="date">
                                                        <abbr class="dtreviewed" title="2018-11-03"> on Nov 3, 2018</abbr>
                                                    </li>
                                                </ul>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="as-community-answer">
                                                <h3 class="as-community-mostusefulanswer">Best Answer:</h3>
                                                <div class="as-community-description">
                                                    <span class=" {{#answers-2}}as-hide{{/answers-2}} ">Sadly, no electronic device can be fully waterproof. The iPhone Xs Max is water-resistant which basi</span>

                                                    <materializer class="as-community-moretext as-moretext more-text" data-render data-uid="answers-2" id="answers-2" {(data-shown)}="answers-2" tabindex="-1">Sadly, no electronic device can be fully waterproof. The iPhone Xs Max is water-resistant which basically means that it can stand water for a specific amount of time. The iPhone Xs Max can be submerged into 2 metres of water for 30 minutes. After that, the phone could be permanently damaged.

Hope this helps!</materializer>

In-store trade-in requires presentation of a valid, government-issued photo ID (local law may require saving this information). Additional terms from Apple or Apple’s trade-in partners may apply. Monthly pricing: Available to qualified customers and requires 0% APR, 24-month installment loan with Citizens One, and iPhone activation with AT&amp;T, Sprint, T-Mobile, or Verizon.  Last installment payment may be less depending on remaining balance. <a href="https://www.apple.com/legal/sales-support/iphoneinstallments_us" target="_blank">Full terms apply</a>.</p>

		<section class="section section-hero" data-analytics-section-engagement="name:hero">
			<div class="section-content row">
				<div class="column hero-hgroup large-8 medium-10 small-12">
					<h1 class="overview-subsection-subheadline eyebrow eyebrow-hero">Apple and ConnectED</h1>
					<h2 class="typography-product-elevated overview-hero-headline">Giving products, support, and opportunities to schools that need them most.</h2>
				</div>
				<div class="column hero-copy large-6 medium-8 small-12 overview-hero-headline">
					<p class="intro typography-intro">Apple has been part of the ConnectED initiative since 2014, pledging $100 million of teaching and learning solutions to 114 underserved schools across the country. We’ve donated an iPad to every student, a Mac and iPad to every teacher, and an Apple TV to every classroom. And we’ve implemented a process that provides planning, professional learning, and ongoing guidance so every school can experience the transformational power of technology.</p>
					<p><a class="hero-cta typography-intro" href="https://www.sri.com/work/publications/apple-and-connected-research-year-2-survey-report">Learn more about the impact of the initiative in SRI Education’s <span class="nowrap icon icon-after icon-external">research report</span></a></p>
				</div>
			</div>
			<div class="hero-gallery zoom-fade-gallery" data-component-list="ZoomFadeGallery">
				<div class="zoom-fade-gallery-item" data-ac-gallery-item>
					<figure class="zoom-fade-gallery-image hero-gallery-image-one" role="img">
						<figcaption class="section-caption caption-copy typography-caption">Nina, Student <span class="css-break">Nanwalek School</span></figcaption>
					</figure>
				</div>
				<div class="zoom-fade-gallery-item" data-ac-gallery-item>
					<figure class="zoom-fade-gallery-image hero-gallery-image-two" role="img">
						<figcaption class="section-caption caption-copy typography-caption">Jacob, Student <span class="css-break">Salida del Sol Elementary School</span></figcaption>
					</figure>
				</div>
				<div class="zoom-fade-gallery-item" data-ac-gallery-item>
					<figure class="zoom-fade-gallery-image hero-gallery-image-three" role="img">
						<figcaption class="section-caption caption-copy typography-caption">Daveon, Student <span class="css-break">Riverview Gardens High School</span></figcaption>
					</figure>
				</div>
			</div>
		</section><!--/.section-hero-->

		<section class="section section-vision" data-analytics-section-engagement="name:vision" >
			<div class="section-content row">
				<div class="column large-6 medium-7 small-12">
					<h2 class="eyebrow eyebrow-hero">Establishing Goals</h2>
					<h3 class="section-headline typography-hero-headline">“We all met to come up with our vision, mission statement, goals, and challenges.”</h3>
					<p>Every school faces unique challenges. That’s why we meet with administrators from each Apple ConnectED school to craft a vision for the role of technology in their classrooms. As part of this planning, we work with school leadership to form a core group of individuals responsible for defining clear and measurable goals.</p>
					<p>At Berkley Campostella Early Childhood Education Center in Norfolk, Virginia, Principal Dr. Doreatha White leads her faculty with a powerful vision — that children are capable of anything if you give them the right tools. “Our motto is: College begins in prekindergarten,” she says. “We have to guide a student’s whole thinking toward being successful beyond pre-K. But to truly start closing the digital divide, we have to get our parents and the community to believe in what we’re doing as well.”</p>
					<p>With that challenge in mind, Dr. White created a community outreach program to help parents understand the transformative power of technology in learning. And one of her first goals was to get 100 percent of the students’ parents to attend How to Use iPad with Your Child workshops, which she achieved with surprising ease. “In the community’s eyes, it was a big thing. We could demonstrate how this would benefit their children and prepare them for lifelong learning. That not only are they doing ABCs and 123s, they’re also learning how to analyze and synthesize instruction. And now they’re excited about learning, which they’ll remember going into kindergarten and beyond.”</p>
					<p>Learn more about Berkley Campostella Early Childhood Center’s journey with ConnectED in a free book written by Principal Dr. Doreatha White.</p>
					<p><a class="icon icon-after icon-external" aria-label='Explore "Berkley Campostella Early Childhood Center” by Dr. Doreatha White on iBooks' href="https://itunes.apple.com/us/book/berkley-campostella-early-childhood-center/id1321563492?mt=11">View on iBooks</a></p>
				</div>
			</div>
			<figure class="image-vision-hero" role="img">
				<figcaption class="section-caption caption-copy typography-caption">Dr. Doreatha White, Principal <span class="css-break">Berkley Campostella Early Childhood Education Center</span></figcaption>
			</figure>
		</section><!--/.section-vision-->

		<section class="section section-infrastructure" data-analytics-section-engagement="name:infrastructure">
			<div class="section-content">
				<div class="row viewport-content">
					<div class="column large-6 medium-8 small-10">
						<h2 class="eyebrow eyebrow-hero">Building Infrastructure</h2>
						<h3 class="section-headline typography-hero-headline">“If you can understand the system, you can maintain it.”</h3>
					</div>
				</div>
				<div class="row viewport-content no-small">
					<div class="viewport-content">
						<div class="column large-6 medium-6 small-12">
							<p>Many Apple ConnectED schools do not have a strong network or a dedicated technology department. So before any products are delivered, Apple Project Engineers conduct a full survey of the school’s existing wireless infrastructure and help install or upgrade a network.</p>
							<p>In the remote village of Nanwalek, Alaska, the K–12 school was making plans to improve its slow, satellite-provided Internet connection. Our engineers consulted with district officials to ensure that the school’s wireless infrastructure would not only be fast, but would also be ready to support the arrival of over 100 new Apple products. In addition to working with the district’s offsite IT team, Apple Project Managers needed to find someone local to handle day-to-day management of the devices. Tommy Evans, an aide and parent in the village, volunteered for the role. “They showed us where a signal goes and how to tailor equipment around students’ needs,” he says. “When things were put in place, it took off like a rocket.”</p>
							<p>The new wireless infrastructure has profoundly affected the school, especially students like Evans’s daughter, Tessie, who is hearing impaired. “Because we’re so isolated, she felt like she was the only one who is deaf.” But soon, Tessie was using FaceTime and other iPad apps to communicate with students and mentors all over the world.</p>
							<p>Learn more about how access to technology connected Nanwalek students to the world beyond their shores in a free book written by Principal Nancy Kleine.</p>
							<p><a class="icon icon-after icon-external" aria-label='Explore “Inspiring New Ways of Learning at Nanwalek School” by Nancy Kleine on iBooks' href="https://itunes.apple.com/us/book/inspiring-new-ways-of-learning-at-nanwalek-school/id1352599192?mt=11">View on iBooks</a></p>
						</div>
					</div>
					<div class="column large-3 small-12 large-offset-1 medium-offset-2 small-offset-0">
						<div class="columns-to-slide-gallery row infrastucture-gallery" data-component-list="ColumnsToSlideGallery" data-ac-gallery-slide>
							<div id="infrastucture-gallery-item-one" class="gallery-item" aria-labelledby="infrastucture-gallery-1" data-ac-gallery-item>
								<figure class="badge">
									<div class="badge-content" role="text">
										<span class="badge-value">760,320</span>
										<span class="badge-caption">feet of Internet cable have been installed in Apple ConnectED schools</span>
									</div>
								</figure>
							</div>
							<div id="infrastucture-gallery-item-two" class="gallery-item" aria-labelledby="infrastucture-gallery-2" data-ac-gallery-item>
								<figure class="badge">
									<div class="badge-content" role="text">
										<span class="badge-value">95</span>
										<span class="badge-normalcase badge-caption">Apple ConnectED schools have received upgrades to their wireless networks since 2014</span>
									</div>
								</figure>
							</div>
							<nav class="dotnav" role="presentation">
								<ul role=“tablist”>
									<li role="presentation"><a role=“tab” id="infrastucture-gallery-1" href="#" class="dotnav-item current" data-ac-gallery-trigger="infrastucture-gallery-item-one"><span class="visuallyhidden">infrastructure gallery item 1</span></a></li>
									<li role="presentation"><a role=“tab” id="infrastucture-gallery-2" href="#" class="dotnav-item" data-ac-gallery-trigger="infrastucture-gallery-item-two"><span class="visuallyhidden">infrastructure gallery item 2</span></a></li>
								</ul>
							</nav>
						</div><!--/gallery-->
					</div>
				</div>
			</div>
			<figure class="image-infrastructure-hero" role="img">
				<figcaption class="section-caption caption-copy typography-caption">Tommy Evans, Aide <span class="css-break">Nanwalek School</span></figcaption>
			</figure>
		</section><!--/.section-infrastructure-->

		<section class="section section-teachers" data-analytics-section-engagement="name:teachers">
			<div class="section-content">
				<div class="row">
					<div class="column large-7 small-12">
						<h2 class="eyebrow eyebrow-hero">Preparing Teachers</h2>
						<h3 class="section-headline typography-hero-headline">“I’ve had to slow down because I get so excited about all you can do.”</h3>
					</div>
				</div>
				<div class="row">
					<div class="column large-6 medium-7 small-12">
						<p>To help every teacher become comfortable with new technology, the Apple Education team provides a series of workshops designed specifically for educators. We start by helping them integrate iPad, Mac, and Apple TV into their curriculum and lessons, then show them how to create original and engaging books, presentations, and other learning materials.</p>
						<p>“Apple made sure not to overwhelm us,” says Kirt Gordon, a third-grade teacher at Salida del Sol Elementary School in Yuma, Arizona. “We could approach each session in small segments, enabling those of us who were further along to advance on our own.”</p>
						<p>Inspired by his professional learning workshops and the agricultural community that surrounds the school, Gordon teaches a lesson about the Archimedes screw, an irrigation device invented in ancient Greece. Using animated simulations in apps, the lesson enables students to rotate iPad for a 3D look at how the machine works so they can create models of their own.</p>
						<p>In 2017, Gordon became part of the Apple Distinguished Educators (ADE) program, which celebrates pioneers of classroom technology. He is one of 13 ConnectED teachers to join the global ADE community.</p>
						<p class="cta"><a class="more" href="/education/apple-distinguished-educator/" data-analytics-region="learn more" data-analytics-title="learn more about apple distinguished educators">Learn more about Apple Distinguished Educators</a></p>
					</div>
					<div class="column large-3 small-12 large-offset-1 medium-offset-2 small-offset-0 badge-column">
						<figure class="badge">
							<div class="badge-content" role="text">
								<span class="badge-value">4,400+</span>
								<span class="badge-normalcase badge-caption">teachers are using iPad in Apple ConnectED schools</span>
							</div>
						</figure>
					</div>
				</div>
			</div>
			<figure class="image-teachers-hero" role="img">
				<figcaption class="section-caption caption-copy typography-caption">Kirt Gordon, Teacher <span class="css-break">Salida del Sol Elementary School</span></figcaption>
			</figure>
		</section><!--/.section-teachers-->

		<section class="section section-students" data-analytics-section-engagement="name:students">
			<figure class="image-students-hero" role="img" aria-labelledby="students-figure-caption"></figure>
			<div class="section-content">
				<div class="row">
					<div class="column large-7 medium-9 small-12">
						<h2 class="eyebrow eyebrow-hero">Delivering Devices to Students</h2>
						<h3 class="section-headline typography-hero-headline">“When something’s on iPad, it’s automatically fun.”</h3>
					</div>
				</div>

				<div class="flex-box">
					<div class="flex-child flex-child-copy-1 large-6 small-12">
						<p>With a strong infrastructure and inspired teachers, schools are ready to put an iPad into each student’s hands.</p>
						<p>All over the country, students at Apple ConnectED schools are using iPad to learn in ways they never could have imagined. Daveon was a ninth-grader at Riverview Gardens High School in St. Louis, Missouri, when he used iMovie on his new iPad to direct a documentary about the misconceptions surrounding his school and community, narrated by teachers and fellow students. Creating the film gave Daveon a way to share his perspective publicly. “It was like I stepped into a new reality,” he said.</p>
					</div>
					<div class="flex-child flex-child-gallery large-5 small-12 large-offset-1 small-offset-0" data-component-list="ModalSlideGallery">
						<div id="students-gallery" class="modal-slide-gallery with-paddlenav with-paddlenav-onhover" data-ac-gallery-slide>
							<div id="students-gallery-1" class="tabpanel" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="students-gallery-1" data-ac-gallery-item>
								<figure class="image-students-gallery-1" aria-labelledby="students-gallery-1-caption" role="img">
									<figcaption id="students-gallery-1-caption" class="caption-copy typography-caption" aria-hidden="true">In Yuma, Arizona, students are using iMovie on iPad to create their own interpretations of a poem.</figcaption>
								</figure>
							</div>
							<div id="students-gallery-2" class="tabpanel" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="students-gallery-2" data-ac-gallery-item>
								<figure class="image-students-gallery-2" aria-labelledby="students-gallery-2-caption" role="img">
									<figcaption id="students-gallery-2-caption" class="caption-copy typography-caption" aria-hidden="true">Students in Nanwalek, Alaska, use iPad to work together on class projects.</figcaption>
								</figure>
							</div>
							<div id="students-gallery-3" class="tabpanel" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="students-gallery-3" data-ac-gallery-item>
								<figure class="image-students-gallery-3" aria-labelledby="students-gallery-3-caption" role="img">
									<figcaption id="students-gallery-3-caption" class="caption-copy typography-caption" aria-hidden="true">Tyrell, a sixth-grader in St. Louis, Missouri, shows his mother an assignment he’s completed on his iPad.</figcaption>
								</figure>
							</div>
							<nav class="dotnav" role="presentation">
								<ul role="tablist">
									<li role="presentation"><a role="tab" id="students-gallery-1" href="#" class="dotnav-item current" data-ac-gallery-trigger="students-gallery-1"><span class="visuallyhidden">student gallery item 1</span></a></li>
									<li role="presentation"><a role="tab" id="students-gallery-2" href="#" class="dotnav-item" data-ac-gallery-trigger="students-gallery-2"><span class="visuallyhidden">student gallery item 2</span></a></li>

								</ul>
							</nav>
							<nav class="paddlenav paddlenav-framed paddlenav-onhover" role="presentation">
								<ul>
									<li><button class="paddlenav-arrow paddlenav-arrow-previous" data-ac-gallery-previous-trigger="students-gallery" aria-label="Previous"></button></li>
									<li><button class="paddlenav-arrow paddlenav-arrow-next" data-ac-gallery-next-trigger="students-gallery" aria-label="Next"></button></li>
								</ul>
							</nav>
						</div>
						<button
						class="modal-trigger-caption caption-copy typography-caption"
						aria-labelledby="students-caption"
						data-modal-trigger
						data-close-aria-text="Close"
						data-modal-aria-text="How students are learning with iPad."

						>
							<figure class="figure-modal-trigger image-students-gallery-thumbnail"></figure>
							<figcaption id="students-caption" class="modal-trigger-caption caption-copy typography-caption"><span class="caption-copy-text">See how students are learning with iPad.</span></figcaption>
						</button>
					</div>
					<div class="flex-child flex-child-copy-2 large-6 small-12">
						<p>In Mr. Nunez’s Language Arts class in Yuma, Arizona, students are learning about rhyme and meter by directing and recording screenplays using GarageBand. Tyrell, who was a sixth-grader at Westview Middle School in St. Louis, created a multimedia presentation in Keynote about the Bahamas after he used Flyover in Maps to take a tour of the islands. And in Nanwalek, Alaska, a student named Severan discovered how important math is in pursuing his dream of being a pilot. He used apps like IXL and Notes to learn about angles and multiplication tables, concepts he planned to put into action flying supplies and people to his village.</p>
					</div>
					<div class="flex-child flex-child-badge large-5 small-12 large-offset-1 small-offset-0">
						<figure class="badge">
							<div class="badge-content" role="text">
								<span class="badge-value">55,000+</span>
								<span class="badge-normalcase badge-caption">students are learning with iPad in Apple ConnectED schools</span>
							</div>

					</div>
				</div>
			</div>
			<figcaption id="students-figure-caption" class="section-caption caption-copy typography-caption" aria-hidden="true">Leondis, Student <span class="css-break">Walton Middle School</span></figcaption>
		</section><!--/.section-students-->

		<section class="section section-support" data-analytics-section-engagement="name:support">
			<div class="section-content">
				<div class="row">
					<div class="column large-7 small-12">
						<h2 class="eyebrow eyebrow-hero">Providing Ongoing Support</h2>
						<h3 class="section-headline typography-hero-headline">“It’s not just ‘Here are the devices, figure out how to use them.’ We’re learning how to do it for life.”</h3>
					</div>
				</div>
				<div class="row">
					<div class="column large-6 medium-7 small-12">
						<p>After each student receives an iPad, we continue building relationships with the schools. Apple Professional Learning Specialists, many of whom are former teachers and maintain teaching certificates, provide administrators, teachers, and students with tailored, onsite support and guidance to help them reach their goals. We also support teachers with online classroom workshops taught by Apple Distinguished Educators and Apple Retail team members. And with Apple Teacher, educators have a free, self-paced learning program to build skills on iPad and Mac.</p>
						<p>At Westview Middle School in St. Louis, Missouri, eighth-grade teacher Brandon Small’s relationship with his Apple Professional Learning Specialist continues to evolve. At first, his APL Specialist was a resource for questions about his new technology. “It was nice sitting down with an expert on Keynote and Pages to learn everything about them,” he remembers. “It gave us something we could use right away in the classroom.”</p>
						<p>Now Small looks to his APL Specialist for ideas to enhance his lessons and his students’ learning. Through a series of workshops, he’s discovering how other apps can help him incorporate interactive games, graphs, and films into his classes. “They’re giving us support and we’re learning. It’s not a one-time thing,” says Small. “The learning keeps getting better.”</p>
						<p><a class="more" href="/education/apple-teacher/" data-analytics-region="learn more" data-analytics-title="learn more about apple teacher">Learn more about Apple Teacher</a></p>
					</div>
					<div class="column large-3 small-12 large-offset-1 medium-offset-2 small-offset-0 badge-column">
						<figure class="badge">
							<div class="badge-content" role="text">
								<span class="badge-value">2,190</span>
								<span class="badge-small badge-caption">days of Apple Professional Learning have been delivered to ConnectED schools since 2014</span>
							</div>
						</figure>
					</div>
				</div>
			</div>
			<figure class="image-support-hero" role="img">
				<figcaption class="section-caption caption-copy typography-caption">Brandon Small, Teacher <span class="css-break">Westview Middle School</span></figcaption>
			</figure>
		</section><!--/.section-support-->

Monthly pricing requires a 24‑month installment loan with a 0% APR, and iPhone activation. Applicable sales tax and fees due at time of purchase. Last payment may be less depending on remaining balance. Additional trade‑in values require purchase of a new iPhone, subject to availability and limits. You must be at least 18 years old. In‑store trade‑in requires presentation of a valid, government‑issued photo ID (local law may require saving this information). Additional terms from Apple or Apple’s trade‑in partners may apply. <a href='/legal/sales-support/iphoneinstallments_us/'>Full terms apply</a>.</li>
